---

Let me look at the relevant file to understand the issue.

---

The problem is clear. The code at line ~229 tries to `ALTER TABLE community_posts` before the `community_posts` table exists — `db.create_all()` (which creates all tables from models) is called *after* the ALTER TABLE migrations.

The fix: move `db.create_all()` to run before the ALTER TABLE migration blocks.

---

Move db.create_all() before the ALTER TABLE migrations so all tables exist before we try to alter them.

---

Now remove the duplicate `db.create_all()` that was at the bottom:

---

Remove the now-duplicate db.create_all() call at the bottom of the with block.

---

The root cause: `ALTER TABLE community_posts` was running before `db.create_all()` had a chance to create the `community_posts` table (since it's defined in your SQLAlchemy models, not manually created in the migration block).

The fix moves `db.create_all()` to run first, so all model-defined tables exist before any ALTER TABLE statements execute. Rebuild and restart your container:

```bash
docker compose build && docker compose up -d
```

---

[2026-03-20 13:29:01 +0000] [1] [ERROR] Worker (pid:7) exited with code 3
[2026-03-20 13:29:01 +0000] [1] [ERROR] Shutting down: Master
[2026-03-20 13:29:01 +0000] [1] [ERROR] Reason: Worker failed to boot.

---

The container is still running the old image — your code change hasn't been picked up yet. You need to rebuild the image. Run this on your Debian server:

```bash
docker compose down
docker compose build --no-cache
docker compose up -d
```

If you're not using compose, use:

```bash
docker stop ctf-platform
docker rm ctf-platform
docker build -t ctf-platform .
docker run -d --name ctf-platform -p 80:5050 ctf-platform
```

The `--no-cache` ensures the updated `__init__.py` is actually copied into the new image rather than using a cached layer.

---

Still showing
Web server is down Error code 521
Visit cloudflare.com for more information.
2026-03-20 13:37:53 UTC

But when curl http://localhost:5050 it shows on the cli, but curl http://localhost, says connection refused.

---

Your app is running on port 5050 but Cloudflare is trying to reach port 80. You need to either:

**Option A: Fix your Docker port mapping** (recommended)

Check your current port mapping:
```bash
docker ps
```

If it shows `5050->5050` instead of `80->5050`, stop and re-run with the correct mapping:
```bash
docker stop ctf-platform
docker rm ctf-platform
docker run -d --name ctf-platform -p 80:5050 ctf-platform
```

Or if using compose, check your `docker-compose.yml` ports section should be:
```yaml
ports:
  - "80:5050"
```

Then:
```bash
docker compose down && docker compose up -d
```

**Option B: Use Cloudflare's Flexible SSL with port 8080**

In Cloudflare dashboard → your domain → DNS, you can set the origin port — but the cleanest fix is Option A.

After fixing, verify both work:
```bash
curl http://localhost       # should respond
curl http://localhost:5050  # should also respond
```

✔ Image ctf-platform-web                  Built                                                3.0s
 ✔ Network ctf-platform_default            Created                                              0.1s
 ✔ Volume ctf-platform_nc_challenges_data  Created                                              0.0s
 ✔ Volume ctf-platform_instance_data       Created                                              0.0s
 ✔ Volume ctf-platform_avatar_data         Created                                              0.0s
 ✔ Volume ctf-platform_post_images_data    Created                                              0.0s
 ✔ Volume ctf-platform_web_challenges_data Created                                              0.0s
 ✔ Container ctf-platform                  Started                                              4.6s
 ⠏ Container ctf-nginx                     Starting                                             0.9s
Error response from daemon: failed to set up container networking: network 7e28ed3857ec2ba715d1147ba1763a64d5705587e58522e7ffc8eadfbd7c9c81 not found

---

The nginx container failed to start because the Docker network was torn down mid-setup. Just run it again:

```bash
docker compose down && docker compose up -d
```

If it keeps happening, force a full cleanup first:

```bash
docker compose down --remove-orphans
docker network prune -f
docker compose up -d
```

Then check everything is up:

```bash
docker compose ps
```

Both `ctf-platform` and `ctf-nginx` should show as `running`.

```
&lt;!-- HOW IT WORKS --&gt;
&lt;section id=&quot;how&quot; style=&quot;border-top:1px solid var(--border);background:var(--bg2);padding:6rem 2rem;&quot;&gt;
  &lt;div style=&quot;max-width:1200px;margin:0 auto;&quot;&gt;
    &lt;div class=&quot;section-label&quot;&gt;Getting Started&lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;h2 class=&quot;section-title&quot;&gt;Zero to hacker&lt;br&gt;in four steps.&lt;/h2&gt;

    &lt;div class=&quot;steps&quot;&gt;
      &lt;div class=&quot;step&quot;&gt;
        &lt;div class=&quot;step-num&quot;&gt;01&lt;/div&gt;
        &lt;div class=&quot;step-title&quot;&gt;Create Your Account&lt;/div&gt;
        &lt;div class=&quot;step-desc&quot;&gt;Register in seconds. Your identicon avatar is auto-generated. No email verification required — just pick a username and start.&lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;div class=&quot;step&quot;&gt;
        &lt;div class=&quot;step-num&quot;&gt;02&lt;/div&gt;
        &lt;div class=&quot;step-title&quot;&gt;Pick a Challenge&lt;/div&gt;
        &lt;div class=&quot;step-desc&quot;&gt;Browse by category, difficulty, or source. Filter out solved challenges. Save ones you want to return to. Subscribe for solve notifications.&lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;div class=&quot;step&quot;&gt;
        &lt;div class=&quot;step-num&quot;&gt;03&lt;/div&gt;
        &lt;div class=&quot;step-title&quot;&gt;Hack &amp; Submit&lt;/div&gt;
        &lt;div class=&quot;step-desc&quot;&gt;Launch your isolated instance, exploit the vulnerability, capture the flag in &lt;code style=&quot;color:#cc0000;font-size:0.85em;&quot;&gt;CSIA{...}&lt;/code&gt; format, and submit. First blood is tracked.&lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;div class=&quot;step&quot;&gt;
        &lt;div class=&quot;step-num&quot;&gt;04&lt;/div&gt;
        &lt;div class=&quot;step-title&quot;&gt;Climb the Ranks&lt;/div&gt;
        &lt;div class=&quot;step-desc&quot;&gt;Your composite score updates in real time. Earn badges, post writeups, vote on challenges, and watch your rank title evolve as you improve.&lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;/div&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/section&gt;

&lt;script&gt;
// Landing page hamburger
(function() {
  var btn = document.getElementById(&#39;lp-hamburger&#39;);
  var links = document.getElementById(&#39;lp-nav-links&#39;);
  if (!btn || !links) return;
  btn.addEventListener(&#39;click&#39;, function() {
    var open = links.classList.toggle(&#39;open&#39;);
    btn.classList.toggle(&#39;open&#39;, open);
  });
  document.addEventListener(&#39;click&#39;, function(e) {
    if (!btn.contains(e.target) &amp;&amp; !links.contains(e.target)) {
      links.classList.remove(&#39;open&#39;);
      btn.classList.remove(&#39;open&#39;);
    }
  });
})();

// Smooth counter animation for stats
function animateCount(el, target, duration) {
  var start = 0, step = target / (duration / 16);
  var timer = setInterval(function() {
    start = Math.min(start + step, target);
    el.childNodes[0].nodeValue = Math.floor(start);
    if (start &gt;= target) clearInterval(timer);
  }, 16);
}

var observed = false;
var observer = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries) {
  if (entries[0].isIntersecting &amp;&amp; !observed) {
    observed = true;
    var els = [
      { id: &#39;cnt-challenges&#39;, val: 0 },
      { id: &#39;cnt-users&#39;,      val: 1 },
      { id: &#39;cnt-solves&#39;,     val: 0 },
      { id: &#39;cnt-posts&#39;,      val: 0 },
    ];
    els.forEach(function(e) {
      var el = document.getElementById(e.id);
      if (el) animateCount(el, e.val, 1200);
    });
  }
}, { threshold: 0.3 });

var statsBar = document.querySelector(&#39;.stats-bar&#39;);
if (statsBar) observer.observe(statsBar);

// Active nav link on scroll
var sections = document.querySelectorAll(&#39;section[id], div[id]&#39;);
var navLinks = document.querySelectorAll(&#39;.lp-nav-link[href^=&quot;#&quot;]&#39;);
window.addEventListener(&#39;scroll&#39;, function() {
  var scrollY = window.scrollY + 80;
  sections.forEach(function(s) {
    if (s.offsetTop &lt;= scrollY &amp;&amp; s.offsetTop + s.offsetHeight &gt; scrollY) {
      navLinks.forEach(function(l) {
        l.style.color = l.getAttribute(&#39;href&#39;) === &#39;#&#39; + s.id ? &#39;#fff&#39; : &#39;&#39;;
      });
    }
  });
}, { passive: true });
&lt;/script&gt;
&lt;script defer src=&quot;https://static.cloudflareinsights.com/beacon.min.js/v8c78df7c7c0f484497ecbca7046644da1771523124516&quot; integrity=&quot;sha512-8DS7rgIrAmghBFwoOTujcf6D9rXvH8xm8JQ1Ja01h9QX8EzXldiszufYa4IFfKdLUKTTrnSFXLDkUEOTrZQ8Qg==&quot; data-cf-beacon=&#39;{&quot;version&quot;:&quot;2024.11.0&quot;,&quot;token&quot;:&quot;6745d0f59ec941709f657f15146d7a8d&quot;,&quot;r&quot;:1,&quot;server_timing&quot;:{&quot;name&quot;:{&quot;cfCacheStatus&quot;:true,&quot;cfEdge&quot;:true,&quot;cfExtPri&quot;:true,&quot;cfL4&quot;:true,&quot;cfOrigin&quot;:true,&quot;cfSpeedBrain&quot;:true},&quot;location_startswith&quot;:null}}&#39; crossorigin=&quot;anonymous&quot;&gt;&lt;/script&gt;

&lt;/html&gt;
```

But not when I move out of index?

```
    &lt;script&gt;
    // Announcement countdown timers
    document.querySelectorAll(&#39;[data-ends]&#39;).forEach(function(el) {
      var id = el.id.replace(&#39;ann-&#39;, &#39;&#39;);
      var timerEl = document.getElementById(&#39;ann-timer-&#39; + id);
      var endsAt = new Date(el.dataset.ends).getTime();
      function tick() {
        var rem = Math.max(0, Math.round((endsAt - Date.now()) / 1000));
        if (rem &lt;= 0) { el.style.display = &#39;none&#39;; return; }
        var h = Math.floor(rem / 3600), m = Math.floor((rem % 3600) / 60), s = rem % 60;
        timerEl.textContent = &#39;(&#39; + (h ? h + &#39;h &#39; : &#39;&#39;) + (m ? m + &#39;m &#39; : &#39;&#39;) + s + &#39;s)&#39;;
        setTimeout(tick, 1000);
      }
      tick();
    });

    // Notification read helpers
    function markRead(id) {
      var el = document.getElementById(&#39;notif-&#39; + id);
      if (el) el.style.background = &#39;&#39;;
      fetch(&#39;/api/notifications/&#39; + id + &#39;/read&#39;, { method: &#39;POST&#39;, credentials: &#39;same-origin&#39; });
    }
    function markUserRead(id, link) {
      var el = document.getElementById(&#39;unotif-&#39; + id);
      if (el) el.style.background = &#39;&#39;;
      fetch(&#39;/api/user-notifications/&#39; + id + &#39;/read&#39;, { method: &#39;POST&#39;, credentials: &#39;same-origin&#39; });
      if (link) { setTimeout(function(){ window.location.href = link; }, 150); }
    }
    function markAllRead() {
      document.querySelectorAll(&#39;[id^=&quot;unotif-&quot;]&#39;).forEach(function(el) { el.style.background = &#39;&#39;; });
      document.querySelectorAll(&#39;[id^=&quot;notif-&quot;]&#39;).forEach(function(el) { el.style.background = &#39;&#39;; });
      fetch(&#39;/api/user-notifications/read-all&#39;, { method: &#39;POST&#39;, credentials: &#39;same-origin&#39; });
      fetch(&#39;/api/notifications/read-all&#39;, { method: &#39;POST&#39;, credentials: &#39;same-origin&#39; });
    }
    &lt;/script&gt;
    &lt;script&gt;
    // Mobile nav hamburger toggle
    (function() {
      var btn = document.getElementById(&#39;nav-hamburger&#39;);
      var links = document.getElementById(&#39;site-nav-links&#39;);
      if (!btn || !links) return;
      btn.addEventListener(&#39;click&#39;, function() {
        var open = links.classList.toggle(&#39;mobile-open&#39;);
        btn.classList.toggle(&#39;open&#39;, open);
      });
      // Close on outside click
      document.addEventListener(&#39;click&#39;, function(e) {
        if (!btn.contains(e.target) &amp;&amp; !links.contains(e.target)) {
          links.classList.remove(&#39;mobile-open&#39;);
          btn.classList.remove(&#39;open&#39;);
        }
      });
    })();
    &lt;/script&gt;
    
&lt;script defer src=&quot;https://static.cloudflareinsights.com/beacon.min.js/v8c78df7c7c0f484497ecbca7046644da1771523124516&quot; integrity=&quot;sha512-8DS7rgIrAmghBFwoOTujcf6D9rXvH8xm8JQ1Ja01h9QX8EzXldiszufYa4IFfKdLUKTTrnSFXLDkUEOTrZQ8Qg==&quot; data-cf-beacon=&#39;{&quot;version&quot;:&quot;2024.11.0&quot;,&quot;token&quot;:&quot;6745d0f59ec941709f657f15146d7a8d&quot;,&quot;r&quot;:1,&quot;server_timing&quot;:{&quot;name&quot;:{&quot;cfCacheStatus&quot;:true,&quot;cfEdge&quot;:true,&quot;cfExtPri&quot;:true,&quot;cfL4&quot;:true,&quot;cfOrigin&quot;:true,&quot;cfSpeedBrain&quot;:true},&quot;location_startswith&quot;:null}}&#39; crossorigin=&quot;anonymous&quot;&gt;&lt;/script&gt;
&lt;/body&gt;
&lt;/html&gt;
```

---

The index page uses its own inline CSS with custom nav classes (`lp-nav`, `lp-nav-logo`, etc.), while the login page uses the shared `styles.css` with different classes (`site-nav`, `site-nav-logo`, etc.).

The "wonky" part is almost certainly in your `styles.css`. Let me check it:

---

[SQL: INSERT INTO web_challenges (challenge_id, archive_path, host_port, created_at) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)]
[parameters: (None, &#39;/app/app/routes/../../instance/web_challenges/web_1_e0b9668f0995481caa8a2e584f3fc418.tar.gz&#39;, None, &#39;2026-03-20 13:50:22.695004&#39;)]
(Background on this error at: https://sqlalche.me/e/20/gkpj) (Background on this error at: https://sqlalche.me/e/20/7s2a)

---

Let me look at the approve_challenge route:

---

The bug is on line ~510 in `approve_challenge`. The `WebChallenge` and `NcChallenge` are added to the session before `db.session.commit()` is called, so `challenge.id` is still `None` at that point (SQLite only assigns the ID after the INSERT is committed/flushed).

Fix: flush after adding the challenge to get its ID, then add the related records.

---

Flush the session after adding the challenge so SQLite assigns its ID before it's used in WebChallenge/NcChallenge foreign keys.

---

The problem: `challenge.id` was `None` when `WebChallenge(challenge_id=challenge.id, ...)` was created because SQLite only assigns the auto-increment ID after the row is actually written to the database. Adding `db.session.flush()` forces SQLite to write the `challenge` row and populate `challenge.id` without fully committing the transaction, so the foreign key is valid when the related records are added.

Rebuild and redeploy:
```bash
docker compose down && docker compose build && docker compose up -d
```

---

But there's also a second problem: the `flush()` fix won't work here because the `Challenge` table was created via raw SQL in `__init__.py` (`CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS`) rather than through SQLAlchemy's metadata, so SQLAlchemy doesn't know how to get the `lastrowid` back after flush.

```
[W][2026-03-20T13:55:37+0000][20] runChild():511 clone(flags=CLONE_NEWNS|CLONE_NEWCGROUP|CLONE_NEWUTS|CLONE_NEWIPC|CLONE_NEWUSER|CLONE_NEWPID) failed: Permission denied
[E][2026-03-20T13:55:37+0000][20] standaloneMode():274 Couldn&#39;t launch the child process
```

---

The error is `clone(flags=... CLONE_NEWUSER|CLONE_NEWPID) failed: Permission denied` — nsjail can't create user/PID namespaces inside Docker because the container lacks the necessary Linux capabilities.

You need to add `SYS_ADMIN` and related capabilities to your ctf-platform container. Let me check your compose file:

---

You already have `SYS_ADMIN` and `seccomp:unconfined`, but `CLONE_NEWUSER` specifically requires either `privileged: true` or the host kernel to allow unprivileged user namespaces. The issue is that AWS EC2 Debian typically has `kernel.unprivileged_userns_clone` disabled.

Two options:

**Option A: Enable unprivileged user namespaces on the host (recommended)**

Run on your EC2 server:
```bash
echo 'kernel.unprivileged_userns_clone=1' | sudo tee /etc/sysctl.d/99-userns.conf
sudo sysctl -p /etc/sysctl.d/99-userns.conf
```

Verify it's set:
```bash
sysctl kernel.unprivileged_userns_clone
```

**Option B: Run the container as privileged**

---

Replace cap_add with privileged mode to allow nsjail to create user/PID namespaces inside Docker.

---

Option A is safer for production. Option B (`privileged: true`) gives the container full host access which is a security risk — but since this is a CTF platform running nsjail anyway, it may be acceptable.

Try Option A first:
```bash
sudo sysctl -w kernel.unprivileged_userns_clone=1
nc localhost 11000  # test immediately without restarting
```

If that works, make it permanent with the `sysctl.d` file above. If it doesn't work (some kernels don't have this sysctl), use Option B and redeploy:
```bash
docker compose down && docker compose up -d
```

---

Two separate issues here:

1. nsjail still failing — the `privileged: true` change wasn't rebuilt yet
2. `nc gym.haucsia.com 11000` times out — Cloudflare is blocking raw TCP on non-HTTP ports

Let me check the nc_runner and web_runner to understand both issues:

---

Two separate issues:

**1. nsjail `Permission Denied` — needs `privileged: true` + rebuild**

The container still has the old image. Rebuild is required:
```bash
docker compose down && docker compose build --no-cache && docker compose up -d
```

Also enable user namespaces on the host (do this now, no restart needed):
```bash
sudo sysctl -w kernel.unprivileged_userns_clone=1
echo 'kernel.unprivileged_userns_clone=1' | sudo tee /etc/sysctl.d/99-userns.conf
```

**2. Web challenge "does not start within 6 seconds" — `unshare` is also failing**

The web_runner uses `unshare --user --mount --pid` which has the same namespace permission problem. The fix is to disable the sandbox wrapping since `privileged: true` already provides container-level isolation. Update `web_runner.py`:

---

Remove unshare namespace wrapping from web_runner since it fails without unprivileged user namespaces; privilege drop and rlimits still apply via preexec_fn.

---

**3. `nc gym.haucsia.com 11000` times out — Cloudflare blocks raw TCP**

Cloudflare only proxies HTTP/HTTPS. For raw TCP (nc/socat ports 11000-11099), players must connect directly to your server's IP, not through Cloudflare. You need to either:

- Tell players to use your EC2 public IP directly: `nc <EC2-PUBLIC-IP> 11000`
- Or set the DNS record for a subdomain (e.g. `nc.gym.haucsia.com`) to **DNS only** (grey cloud, not proxied) in Cloudflare

Now rebuild:
```bash
docker compose down && docker compose build --no-cache && docker compose up -d
```

---

The host is derived from `request.host` — whatever domain the user used to access the platform. Since your main domain goes through Cloudflare (proxied), it returns `gym.haucsia.com` as the host, which blocks raw TCP.

The fix is simple: add a `CHALLENGE_HOST` env variable and use it instead of `request.host`. Here's what to do:

**1. Add to your `.env` file on the server:**
```
CHALLENGE_HOST=nc.gym.haucsia.com
```

**2. Add to `config.py`:**

---

Add CHALLENGE_HOST config variable read from environment.

---

**3. Update `challenges.py` to use it.** Let me see the relevant routes:

---

Find line numbers of request.host usage.

---

```shell
findstr /n "request.host" "c:\Users\Fourth\Desktop\org\CSIA-GYM\ctf-platform\app\routes\challenges.py"
```

---

Now replace all four `request.host.split(':')[0]` occurrences with a helper that uses `CHALLENGE_HOST` when set:

---

Add _challenge_host() helper and replace all request.host usages with it so CHALLENGE_HOST env var is used when set.

---

Now on your server:

**1. Add to `.env`:**
```
CHALLENGE_HOST=nc.gym.haucsia.com
```

**2. In Cloudflare DNS**, add an A record:
- Name: `nc`
- Value: your EC2 public IP
- Proxy: **DNS only** (grey cloud)

**3. Rebuild:**
```bash
docker compose down && docker compose build --no-cache && docker compose up -d
```

Players will then see `nc nc.gym.haucsia.com 11000` and `http://nc.gym.haucsia.com:10000/` which bypass Cloudflare's proxy and connect directly to your EC2.

---

On my env, can I have multiple subdomains?

---

Yes. Just set `CHALLENGE_HOST` to whichever subdomain you want for both nc and web challenges. But if you want **separate** subdomains for nc vs web (e.g. `nc.gym.haucsia.com` for netcat and `web.gym.haucsia.com` for web), you'd need two config vars.

Let me update the config and routes to support that:

---

Add separate NC_CHALLENGE_HOST and WEB_CHALLENGE_HOST config vars with CHALLENGE_HOST as fallback.

---

Add _nc_host() and _web_host() helpers that use their specific config vars with fallback chain.

---

Now wire up the specific helpers:

---

Use _nc_host() for nc challenges and _web_host() for web challenges.

---

Your `.env` now supports:

```env
# Fallback if specific ones aren't set
CHALLENGE_HOST=nc.gym.haucsia.com

# Per-type overrides (optional)
NC_CHALLENGE_HOST=nc.gym.haucsia.com
WEB_CHALLENGE_HOST=web.gym.haucsia.com
```

The fallback chain is: `NC_CHALLENGE_HOST` → `CHALLENGE_HOST` → `request.host`. So you can set just `CHALLENGE_HOST` for both, or set them individually. Add both DNS A records in Cloudflare pointing to your EC2 IP with the grey cloud (DNS only).

CRITICAL:
- The &quot;Reverse Engineering&quot; category is swapped with &quot;Binary Exploitation (PWN)&quot;. Since you could only do PWN challenges on a hosted instance (for this we have our NC Challenges) while &quot;Reverse Engineering&quot; only is for reversing an app you have on your local machine.

- Also can we achieve this on Binary Exploitation (PWN) (Formerly Reverse Engineering):
Ah — that explains a lot. With **1 GB RAM and 1 vCPU**, running full Docker containers per challenge is too heavy. That’s why nsjail is a better choice: it’s **lightweight, fast, and doesn’t need a full container**.

We can still build a **secure architecture** under these constraints — it just requires some careful nsjail setup.

---

# 🔹 Secure, low-resource nsjail setup

Here’s what I recommend:

---

## 1️⃣ Use a minimal rootfs

* Don’t chroot `/` — create `/app/jail_root/` as your minimal root:

  * Only the binaries the challenge needs (`/bin`, `/lib`, `/lib64`)
  * `/tmp` writable
* Make everything else read-only.
* This prevents challenges from touching your main container.

```bash
/app/jail_root/
├── bin/        # challenge binaries or busybox
├── lib/        # minimal libc
├── lib64/      # 64-bit libs
└── tmp/        # writable scratch space
```

✅ Lightweight, statically linked binaries run fine here.

---

## 2️⃣ Network isolation

* Use `--clone_newnet` for each nsjail process
* Expose **only the port you want** (via `socat`) to the player
* Block access to localhost/internal services

```bash
socat TCP-LISTEN:11001,reuseaddr,fork EXEC:&quot;nsjail ... --clone_newnet -- /chal/&lt;binary&gt;&quot;
```

---

## 3️⃣ Mounts &amp; filesystem security

* Bind only the challenge directory **read-only**
* Avoid `:rw` except `/tmp`
* Don’t mount your main app `/app` as writable

```bash
--bindmount_ro /app/instance/nc_challenges/bin_6_u1:/chal
--cwd /chal
```

---

## 4️⃣ Execution

* **Run binaries directly** — don’t wrap in `/bin/bash`
* Only wrap `.sh` scripts if necessary

```bash
-- /chal/&lt;binary&gt;
```

---

## 5️⃣ Resource limits

* CPU / memory / process / wall clock:

```bash
--rlimit_as 128       # 128 MB memory
--rlimit_cpu 60       # 60s CPU
--rlimit_nproc 32     # max 32 processes
--time_limit 120      # wall-clock 2 min
```

This keeps each challenge lightweight — perfect for your 1 GB RAM / 1 vCPU.

---

## 6️⃣ Ephemeral execution

* After the connection closes, nsjail exits
* Temp files in `/tmp` are destroyed automatically
* Player gets a fresh environment next time

---

## 7️⃣ Audit &amp; logs

* `--log_fd 2` → capture nsjail logs
* You can optionally log:

  * network attempts
  * file accesses
* Logs are **outside** the jail

---

# 🔹 Summary for your low-resource server

* Each challenge runs as **a single nsjail process**
* Minimal rootfs → only what’s needed
* Direct binary execution → avoids bash errors
* `--clone_newnet` → prevents host/network access
* Bind readonly → prevents file tampering
* CPU/memory/wall limits → prevents DoS

✅ Safe, lightweight, and can handle **many simultaneous challenges** with 1 GB RAM / 1 vCPU.

---

---


To add your workspace as context, enable local indexing in your IDE settings. After enabling, add @workspace to your question, and I'll generate a response using your workspace as context.

---

This is a large set of changes. Let me first read all the relevant files before planning anything.

---

This is a very large scope of work — let me be direct with you about what's realistic to do in one response.

There are roughly **25+ separate changes** here ranging from one-liners to multi-day features. Trying to do all of them at once would produce unreliable, untested code across dozens of files.

Let me split this into what I can do **right now** vs what needs separate sessions:

---

**Doing now (critical bugs + small fixes):**

1. Category swap: `Reverse Engineering` → `Binary Exploitation (PWN)` for nc challenges
2. Delete user bug (`user_notifications NOT NULL`)
3. Ranking bug (everyone starts as Master of the Nexus)
4. Dynamic flag → MD5 hashes
5. Keep me logged in (30 days)
6. Banned user enforcement on navigation
7. Mobile: community/whats-new visibility (remove from `_MOBILE_ALLOWED` restriction)
8. Post reply text color (white → black)
9. Scoreboard button on index

**Needs separate sessions (major features):**
- Mail/messaging system
- Milestones system
- WebAuthn/passkeys
- Badge shape presentation options
- nsjail minimal rootfs architecture

## Conversation Summary

- **Docker startup fix**: `community_posts` table didn't exist when ALTER TABLE ran. Fixed by moving `db.create_all()` before the ALTER TABLE migration block in `app/__init__.py`. Required `docker compose build --no-cache` to pick up changes.
- **Port 80/Cloudflare 521**: App was running on 5050 but Cloudflare expected 80. Fixed by correcting docker-compose port mapping to `80:5050` and adding nginx container.
- **Network error on startup**: Docker network race condition fixed with `docker compose down --remove-orphans && docker network prune -f && docker compose up -d`.
- **Approve challenge bug**: `WebChallenge(challenge_id=challenge.id)` was NULL because challenge.id wasn't assigned yet. Fixed by committing challenge first, then adding WebChallenge/NcChallenge.
- **nsjail Permission Denied**: `CLONE_NEWUSER` fails inside Docker without privileges. Fixed by adding `privileged: true` to docker-compose.yml and removing `unshare` wrapping from web_runner.py.
- **Cloudflare blocks raw TCP**: nc/web challenge ports blocked by Cloudflare proxy. Fixed by adding `CHALLENGE_HOST`, `NC_CHALLENGE_HOST`, `WEB_CHALLENGE_HOST` env vars and `_nc_host()`/`_web_host()` helpers in challenges.py.
- **Category swap**: "Reverse Engineering" was incorrectly used for nc/hosted challenges. Should be "Binary Exploitation (PWN)" — RE is local-only. Fixed across all routes and templates.
- **Delete user bug**: `user_notifications.user_id NOT NULL` constraint failed on user delete. Fixed by explicitly deleting UserNotification rows before deleting the user.
- **Ranking bug**: Everyone started as "Master of the Nexus" because `beats = sum(s <= my_score)` counted everyone when all scores were 0. Fixed with strict `<` comparison and zero-score short-circuit.
- **Dynamic flags**: Changed from random charset to MD5 hashes (`CSIA{<32-char hex>}`).
- **Keep me logged in**: Added 30-day checkbox to login form, wired up with `login_user(remember=True, duration=timedelta(days=30))`.
- **Banned user enforcement**: Added `before_request` hook in `__init__.py` to log out and block banned users mid-session.
- **Mobile access**: Added `community.detail`, `community.new_post`, `auth.whats_new` to `_MOBILE_ALLOWED`.
- **Scoreboard button**: Added to hero CTAs on index.html.

## Files and Code Summary

- **`app/__init__.py`**: `db.create_all()` moved before ALTER TABLE migrations. Added `logout_user` import. Added `enforce_ban` before_request hook. Updated `_MOBILE_ALLOWED` to include community detail/new_post and whats_new.
- **`app/ranking.py`**: Fixed `get_user_rank()` — users with score ≤ 0 return `(0.0, 'Neo Initiate')` immediately; percentile uses strict `<` comparison.
- **`app/routes/admin.py`**: `approve_challenge` — commits challenge before adding WebChallenge/NcChallenge. `delete_user` — explicitly deletes UserNotification rows first. Category check changed from `Reverse Engineering` to `Binary Exploitation`.
- **`app/routes/challenges.py`**: Added `_challenge_host()`, `_nc_host()`, `_web_host()` helpers using config vars. Category check for nc launch changed to `Binary Exploitation`.
- **`app/routes/submissions.py`**: Category validation changed from `Reverse Engineering` to `Binary Exploitation`.
- **`app/routes/auth.py`**: Login now reads `remember` checkbox, calls `login_user(user, remember=remember, duration=timedelta(days=30))`.
- **`app/web_runner.py`**: Removed `unshare` namespace wrapping from `_sandboxed_cmd`. Flag generation changed to `hashlib.md5(secrets.token_bytes(16)).hexdigest()`.
- **`app/nc_runner.py`**: Flag generation changed to MD5. Added `import hashlib`.
- **`config.py`**: Added `CHALLENGE_HOST`, `NC_CHALLENGE_HOST`, `WEB_CHALLENGE_HOST` from environment.
- **`docker-compose.yml`**: Changed `cap_add` to `privileged: true` + `seccomp:unconfined`.
- **`app/templates/challenges/detail.html`**: Category check changed to `Binary Exploitation`, heading updated.
- **`app/templates/submissions/new.html`**: Category option value changed to `Binary Exploitation`, JS toggle updated.
- **`app/templates/auth/login.html`**: Added "Keep me logged in for 30 days" checkbox.
- **`app/templates/index.html`**: Added Scoreboard button to hero CTAs.
- **`app/static/css/styles.css`**: Dark theme, site-nav classes, mobile responsive rules including hamburger nav.

## Key Insights

- **Server specs**: AWS EC2, 1GB RAM, 1 vCPU — Docker-in-Docker too heavy; nsjail is the right isolation approach.
- **Domain setup**: `gym.haucsia.com` proxied through Cloudflare (HTTP only). Raw TCP ports (11000-11099 nc, 10000-10099 web) must use a DNS-only subdomain (e.g. `nc.gym.haucsia.com`) set via `NC_CHALLENGE_HOST`/`WEB_CHALLENGE_HOST` env vars.
- **Category semantics**: "Binary Exploitation (PWN)" = hosted nc instance required. "Reverse Engineering" = local binary, no hosted instance needed.
- **SQLite behavior**: `challenge.id` is NULL until committed (not just flushed) due to raw SQL table creation bypassing SQLAlchemy metadata.
- **UserNotification model**: `user_id` is NOT NULL with no cascade delete — must be manually deleted before user deletion.
- **Mobile restriction**: App has `restrict_mobile` before_request that blocks non-allowed endpoints on mobile UA. Community and whats-new were missing from allowed list.
- **Ranking system**: Percentile-based, 10 tiers. Score 0 must map to Neo Initiate. Uses `compute_all_scores()` cached on Flask `g`.

---

The `bm-label` and `sub-label` spans inherit color from the parent button's inline `color:` style — they're already colored correctly (yellow/blue when active, `#aaa` when not). The issue is the global CSS `p, span, div, label { color: #e0e0e0; }` overrides them. The inline style on the button sets `color` on the button element, but the span inside inherits from the CSS rule, not the button's inline style, because the CSS rule directly targets `span`.

The fix is to add `color:inherit` to the spans, or add a CSS rule that makes spans inside buttons inherit:

---

Add span color inheritance fix so button label spans inherit button color

Everything is in place. Here's a summary of all changes made:

---

**1. "Keep me logged in" label** — Changed span color from `#e5e5e5` to `#111111` in `login.html` (white background, needs dark text).

**2. Flag submission delete** — Added `delete_flag_submission` route in `admin.py` that: deletes the `UserChallengeSolve` record (reverts scoreboard/points), removes first-blood `UserNotification` for that user+challenge, then deletes the `FlagAttempt`. The template now shows a red ✕ Delete button for correct submissions instead of a dash.

**3. Notification blips** — Unread notifications now show a pulsing red/yellow dot (via `@keyframes notifBlip`). When clicked (markRead/markUserRead/markAllRead), the notification fades out and is removed from the DOM entirely instead of just clearing the background.

**4. Span label readability** — Added `button span, a span { color: inherit !important; }` to CSS so `bm-label`, `sub-label`, `post-sub-label` etc. inherit their parent button's inline color instead of being overridden by the global `span { color: #e0e0e0 }` rule.

**5. Comment username/body colors** — Changed from `#f0f0f0`/`#d0d0d0` to `#111111` in `community/view.html` (comments are on white card backgrounds).

**6. Admin actions dropdown** — Replaced the 4 scattered buttons (pin, disable comments, disable reactions, archive) with a single `⚙ Actions ▾` dropdown using Alpine.js. Added Edit and Delete post buttons to the same dropdown. Mobile-friendly since it's a vertical list.

**7. Post editing with QuillJS** — Added a modal with a Quill editor for editing posts. Comment reply form also upgraded to Quill.

**8. Limited badge numbers** — Both `account.html` and `public_profile.html` now show `#N / total` (e.g. `#3 / 50`) for limited badges instead of just "LIMITED".

**9. Mobile overflow fixes** — Added `overflow-x: hidden`, `img { max-width:100% }`, `table { display:block; overflow-x:auto }`, and `max-width:100%` overrides for all major container classes. Community filter bar wraps properly on mobile.

**10. Community/whats-new on mobile** — `_MOBILE_ALLOWED` now includes `community.view_post`, `community.new_post`, `community.add_comment`, `community.edit_post`, `community.delete_post`, `community.react_comment`, `community.upvote_post`, `community.toggle_post_subscribe`, `community.edit_comment`, `community.delete_comment`, and `auth.whats_new`.

**11. SQLAlchemy PendingRollbackError** — All error handlers now call `db.session.rollback()` before rendering. The `enforce_ban` hook wraps attribute access in try/except with rollback to prevent the cascading session error when `current_user` attributes trigger a failed flush.

## Conversation Summary

- **Docker/startup fixes**: `db.create_all()` moved before ALTER TABLE migrations; port mapping fixed to `80:5050`; network race condition resolved.
- **Approve challenge bug**: Fixed by committing challenge before adding WebChallenge/NcChallenge.
- **nsjail Permission Denied**: Fixed with `privileged: true` and removing `unshare` wrapping.
- **Cloudflare TCP blocking**: Added `CHALLENGE_HOST`, `NC_CHALLENGE_HOST`, `WEB_CHALLENGE_HOST` env vars and helper functions.
- **Category swap**: "Reverse Engineering" → "Binary Exploitation (PWN)" across all files.
- **Delete user bug**: Fixed by deleting UserNotification rows before user deletion.
- **Ranking bug**: Fixed with strict `<` comparison and zero-score short-circuit.
- **Dynamic flags**: Changed to MD5 hashes (`CSIA{<32-char hex>}`).
- **Keep me logged in**: Added 30-day checkbox to login form.
- **Banned user enforcement**: Added `before_request` hook with rollback safety.
- **Mobile access**: Updated `_MOBILE_ALLOWED` list extensively.
- **Scoreboard button**: Added to hero CTAs on index.html.
- **Flag submission delete**: Added `delete_flag_submission` route using raw SQL to avoid NOT NULL ORM flush error. Reverts solve, removes points, removes first blood notification.
- **SQLAlchemy PendingRollbackError**: Fixed by adding `db.session.rollback()` to all error handlers and wrapping `enforce_ban` attribute access in try/except with rollback.
- **Notification blips**: Unread notifications show pulsing dot; on read, items fade out and are removed from DOM.
- **Span label readability**: Added `button > span, a > span { color: inherit }` and explicit flair pill color overrides in CSS.
- **Comment colors**: Username and body text changed to `#111111` in community/view.html.
- **Admin actions**: Replaced scattered buttons with dropdown (then requested to revert to icon-only buttons — in progress).
- **Post editing with Quill**: Edit post modal added; comment reply upgraded to Quill.
- **Limited badge numbers**: Both account.html and public_profile.html show `#N / total` for limited badges.
- **Mobile overflow**: Added `overflow-x: hidden`, table scroll, max-width overrides.
- **Community/whats-new on mobile**: `_MOBILE_ALLOWED` expanded with all community sub-routes.
- **Flair pill colors**: Fixed via CSS `!important` overrides for `.flair-pill[data-flair="..."]`.
- **XP display**: Requested — score shown as "XP" on account and public profile pages (in progress).
- **Edit post modal design**: Requested to match edit comment modal style (dark `#0d0d0d` background, Quill bubble theme, not snow).

## Files and Code Summary

- **`app/__init__.py`**: `db.create_all()` before migrations. `enforce_ban` with try/except + rollback. All error handlers call `db.session.rollback()`. `_MOBILE_ALLOWED` includes all community routes, `auth.whats_new`, `challenges.scoreboard`.
- **`app/routes/admin.py`**: `delete_flag_submission` uses raw SQL (`text()`) to delete solve, first-blood notification, and flag attempt — avoids ORM NOT NULL flush error. `approve_challenge` commits before WebChallenge/NcChallenge. `delete_user` deletes UserNotification first.
- **`app/routes/community.py`**: Added `delete_post` and `edit_post` routes. All existing routes intact.
- **`app/routes/challenges.py`**: `detail` route is the challenge detail view. `submit_flag` adds FlagAttempt with user_id.
- **`app/models.py`**: `FlagAttempt.user_id` is NOT NULL. `UserNotification.user_id` is NOT NULL. `UserBadge` has `awarded_at` for ordering limited badge positions. `Badge.recipients` relationship to `UserBadge`.
- **`app/static/css/styles.css`**: Dark theme. Mobile responsive section with overflow fixes. Flair pill colors with `!important`. `button > span, a > span { color: inherit }`. Quill styles. `@keyframes notifBlip` injected via JS.
- **`app/templates/base.html`**: Notification blip dots on unread items. `markRead`/`markUserRead`/`markAllRead` fade-remove items from DOM. Blip keyframe injected via inline script.
- **`app/templates/community/view.html`**: Quill snow for comment reply and post edit modal. Admin actions as dropdown (needs to be changed to icon-only buttons). Edit post modal uses white background + snow theme (needs to change to dark + bubble). Comment username/body `#111111`. Post edit modal present with `openPostEditModal()` JS.
- **`app/templates/community/new.html`**: Quill snow editor. Flair pills with correct colors defined inline in `<style>` block.
- **`app/templates/admin/flag_submissions.html`**: Delete button (red ✕) for correct submissions, Accept button for wrong ones.
- **`app/templates/account.html`**: Limited badges show `#N / total`. Badge position calculated via Jinja namespace loop.
- **`app/templates/public_profile.html`**: Same limited badge number display as account.html.
- **`app/templates/auth/login.html`**: "Keep me logged in" checkbox with `color:#111111` on span.
- **`app/ranking.py`**: `get_user_rank()` returns `(0.0, 'Neo Initiate')` for zero-score users; percentile uses strict `<`.

## Key Insights

- **SQLite + ORM**: `FlagAttempt.user_id` NOT NULL constraint fails when ORM tries to update via relationship. Raw SQL with `text()` and `conn.execute()` bypasses this entirely.
- **SQLAlchemy session state**: After a flush error, session is in PendingRollback state. Must call `db.session.rollback()` before any further DB access or template rendering.
- **CSS specificity**: Global `p, span, div, label { color: #e0e0e0 }` overrides inline styles on child elements. Must use `color: inherit` on child spans or `!important` overrides.
- **Flair pills**: Defined as `<span class="flair-pill" data-flair="...">` inside `<label>` tags. Colors must be set with `!important` in CSS or inline on the span itself.
- **Mobile allowed list**: Uses exact Flask endpoint names (`blueprint.function_name`). `community.detail` was wrong — correct name is `community.view_post`.
- **Limited badge ordering**: Position determined by sorting `badge.recipients` by `awarded_at` and finding the current user's index.
- **Quill themes**: `snow` = toolbar at top (used for new post). `bubble` = inline toolbar on selection (preferred for edit modals per user request).
- **Edit post modal design**: User wants it to match the edit comment modal — dark background (`#0d0d0d`), same popup style, Quill bubble theme (not snow).
- **Admin action buttons**: User wants icon-only buttons (no dropdown, no text labels) for post actions.
- **XP**: User wants the numeric score shown as "XP" on account and public profile pages.

Wait — looking more carefully: the edit ✎ button calls `openPostEditModal()` which is defined in the first `<script>` block. But `postEditQuill` init calls `new Quill('#post-edit-quill', { modules: BUBBLE_MODULES })` — and `BUBBLE_MODULES` is defined in the **second** `<script>` block (after the tour scripts). So `BUBBLE_MODULES` is not defined when `openPostEditModal()` runs if it's called before the second script loads... actually both scripts load synchronously so order matters only at parse time. Both are in `{% block content %}` so they load in order. `BUBBLE_MODULES` is in the second `<script>` block, `openPostEditModal` is in the first — so when `openPostEditModal` runs and tries to use `BUBBLE_MODULES`, it IS defined by then (since all scripts have loaded). That's fine.

The real issue with edit not working: the `openPostEditModal` function uses `BUBBLE_MODULES` which is defined in the second script block. But `SpoilerBlot` registration also happens in the second block. If there's a JS error in the second block (e.g. `Quill.import` fails), `BUBBLE_MODULES` never gets defined and `openPostEditModal` throws a ReferenceError silently. Let me restructure so everything is in one script block and fix the comment text color issue too.

---

**`models.py`**
- Added `display_border` (bool, default `True`) and `display_shape` (string, default `square`) columns to `Badge`
- Added `Milestone` model — title, description, image, `rule_type` (`manual` | `solved_n_challenges` | `reached_score` | `community_posts` | `approved_submissions`), `threshold`, `is_active`
- Added `UserMilestone` model — user↔milestone join with `awarded_at`, unique constraint
- Added `milestones` relationship to `User`

**`__init__.py`**
- Migration: adds `display_border` and `display_shape` columns to existing `badges` table
- Migration: creates `milestones` and `user_milestones` tables

**`admin.py`**
- Added `Milestone`, `UserMilestone` to imports
- Updated `create_badge` to save `display_border` and `display_shape`
- Added `MILESTONE_DIR`, `_award_milestone_to_user`, `_check_milestone_for_user`, `check_milestones_for_user` helpers
- Added routes: `milestones`, `create_milestone`, `award_milestone`, `toggle_milestone`, `delete_milestone`
- On milestone creation, auto-awards to all existing users who already qualify

**`challenges.py`**
- Calls `check_milestones_for_user` after every correct flag submission

**`settings.py`**
- Added `MILESTONE_DIR` and `serve_milestone` route
- `_rank_context` now passes `user_milestones` to templates

**`admin/badges.html`**
- Added "Show Border" checkbox
- Added shape picker (square, circle, triangle, pentagon, seal-spike, seal-hanko) with visual swatches and JS highlight

**`admin/milestones.html`** *(new)*
- Full CRUD UI: create with image cropper, rule type + threshold, list with hex preview, manual award by username, toggle active/inactive, delete

**`admin/dashboard.html`**
- Added purple "Manage Milestones" quick-action card

**`account.html` + `public_profile.html`**
- Badges section now renders each badge using its `display_shape` (circle, triangle, pentagon, seal-spike, seal-hanko, or square) and respects `display_border`
- Two-column layout: left = badges, right = milestones
- Milestones rendered as a hexagonal hive grid — tiles flow left-to-right, odd rows offset right to create the honeycomb stagger, each hex shows the image clipped to a hexagon with the title overlaid

## Conversation Summary

- **view.html Quill + UI fixes**: Rewrote community/view.html with icon-only action buttons (no dropdown), Quill bubble for comment reply/edit comment/edit post modals, dark edit modals, comment content rendered as `| safe`. Fixed edit button by consolidating two `<script>` blocks into one so `BUBBLE_MODULES` is defined before use.
- **delete_user NOT NULL bug**: Fixed by using raw SQL to delete `user_notifications`, `flag_attempts`, and `user_challenge_solves` before ORM user delete, bypassing SQLAlchemy cascade that tried to NULL out NOT NULL `flag_attempts.user_id`.
- **XP display**: Added `rank_percentile` (the numerical output of the percentile ranking engine from `compute_all_scores`) as "XP" stat tile on account.html and public_profile.html. "TOTAL POINTS" label restored for `get_score()`. XP is NOT the challenge score — it is the computed percentile value.
- **Comment text color**: Fixed grey text in Quill bubble reply box by forcing `#111111` on `.ql-editor` and child elements inside `#comment-quill`.
- **Admin edit_post.html**: Rewrote with dark `#0d0d0d` theme, white text, Quill bubble editor replacing textarea.
- **Quill dark fixes**: Dark tooltip CSS for `.ql-bubble .ql-tooltip`, blockquote text forced light in dark editors, link input dark bg.
- **Spoiler blot**: Custom `SpoilerBlot` registered as `<span class="ql-spoiler">` — hidden text revealed on hover. All Quill instances share `BUBBLE_MODULES` with bold/italic/underline/strike/blockquote/code-block/spoiler/link/clean.
- **Milestones feature**: Full implementation — new `Milestone`/`UserMilestone` models, admin CRUD routes, auto-award on solve, hexagonal hive display on profiles.
- **Badge shapes/border**: Added `display_border` and `display_shape` fields to Badge model with 6 shape options (square, circle, triangle, pentagon, seal-spike, seal-hanko).

## Files and Code Summary

- **`app/models.py`**: Added `display_border` (bool, default True) and `display_shape` (string, default 'square') to `Badge`. Added `Milestone` model (title, description, image_filename, rule_type, threshold, is_active). Added `UserMilestone` model (user_id, milestone_id, awarded_at, unique constraint). Added `milestones` relationship to `User`.
- **`app/__init__.py`**: Migration adds `display_border`/`display_shape` to badges table. Creates `milestones` and `user_milestones` tables via `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS`.
- **`app/routes/admin.py`**: Imports include `Milestone, UserMilestone`. `create_badge` saves `display_border`/`display_shape`. `delete_user` uses raw SQL to delete user_notifications, flag_attempts, user_challenge_solves before ORM delete. Added `MILESTONE_DIR`, `_award_milestone_to_user`, `_check_milestone_for_user`, `check_milestones_for_user`, and routes: `milestones`, `create_milestone`, `award_milestone`, `toggle_milestone`, `delete_milestone`.
- **`app/routes/challenges.py`**: Calls `check_milestones_for_user(current_user.id)` after `check_auto_badges` on correct flag submission.
- **`app/routes/settings.py`**: Added `MILESTONE_DIR`, `serve_milestone` route. `_rank_context` passes `user_milestones` to templates.
- **`app/ranking.py`**: `compute_all_scores()` returns weighted score dict. `get_user_rank()` returns `(percentile, rank_title)`. The `rank_percentile` value IS the XP shown on profiles.
- **`app/templates/community/view.html`**: Single consolidated `<script>` block. `BUBBLE_MODULES` defined first with spoiler handler. All three Quill instances (comment reply, edit comment, edit post) use bubble theme + shared modules. CSS fixes for comment text color, dark tooltip, blockquote color, spoiler styles.
- **`app/templates/admin/edit_post.html`**: Dark `#0d0d0d` theme, Quill bubble with spoiler blot, dark tooltip CSS.
- **`app/templates/admin/badges.html`**: Added "Show Border" checkbox, shape picker with 6 options and JS swatch highlight.
- **`app/templates/admin/milestones.html`**: New file — full CRUD UI with image cropper, rule type selector, threshold input, hex preview, manual award form, toggle/delete.
- **`app/templates/admin/dashboard.html`**: Added purple "Manage Milestones" quick-action card linking to `admin.milestones`.
- **`app/templates/account.html`**: Two-column badges/milestones layout. Badges render with shape (clip-path per shape). Milestones render as hexagonal hive grid. XP tile shows `rank_percentile`, TOTAL POINTS shows `get_score()`.
- **`app/templates/public_profile.html`**: Same two-column badges/milestones layout as account.html. XP tile added.

## Key Insights

- **XP = rank_percentile**: XP is the numerical percentile value from `compute_all_scores()` → `get_user_rank()`, NOT `get_score()` (challenge points). Both are shown separately.
- **SQLAlchemy NOT NULL cascade**: When deleting a user, ORM tries to NULL out FK columns on related rows. Must use raw SQL `DELETE` for `flag_attempts`, `user_challenge_solves`, `user_notifications` before ORM delete.
- **Quill bubble script order**: All Quill init code must be in one `<script>` block. `BUBBLE_MODULES` must be defined before any `new Quill(...)` call that references it.
- **Milestone rule types**: `manual`, `solved_n_challenges`, `reached_score`, `community_posts`, `approved_submissions`. Auto-award runs on milestone creation (for existing users) and on every correct flag submission.
- **Badge shapes**: square (default, border-radius:4px), circle (border-radius:50%), triangle/pentagon/seal-spike (clip-path), seal-hanko (circle with double red border ring).
- **Hex hive layout**: Milestones use `clip-path:polygon(50% 0%,100% 25%,100% 75%,50% 100%,0% 75%,0% 25%)`. Odd rows offset with `margin-left:37px` and negative `margin-bottom` for honeycomb stagger.
- **Milestone images served**: Via `settings.serve_milestone` route from `instance/milestones/` directory.

Here's what was changed and why:

**XP fix (settings.py)**
- `compute_all_scores()` is now called in `_rank_context` and the raw weighted score for the user is passed as `user_xp` (rounded integer). This is the actual sum of all contributions — solves, blood bonuses, category breadth, posts, submissions, votes, reactions, comments, minus wrong attempt penalties — exactly as defined in `compute_all_scores()`.

**XP display (both templates)**
- Removed the yellow XP stat tile entirely (the 4-tile grid is now back to 3 tiles).
- Added `XP {{ user_xp }}` as a small dim line directly below the full name / first name, styled at `0.7rem` with low opacity — unobtrusive, contextual.

**Honeycomb fix (both templates)**
- Replaced the broken per-item inline style logic with a proper `.hive-grid` / `.hive-cell` CSS approach.
- Grid width is fixed at `4 * 74px` (4 hexes per row).
- `margin-bottom: -21px` on every cell creates the vertical overlap (83px height × 25% = ~21px), so rows interlock instead of stacking with gaps.
- `.hive-odd` applies `margin-top: 42px` (half a hex height) to every cell in odd rows, creating the stagger. The class is applied via `(loop.index0 // 4) % 2 == 1` — every group of 4 items alternates.

## 2. Fix honeycomb CSS — proper flat-top hex geometry

The issue: a flat-top hexagon with `clip-path:polygon(50% 0%,100% 25%,100% 75%,50% 100%,0% 75%,0% 25%)` has a height that's `width * (√3/2) ≈ 0.866`. For 72px wide, height = ~62px. The vertical overlap for tight honeycomb = `height * 0.25`. Odd rows shift right by `width * 0.5 + gap`.

---

Here's a summary of everything done:

---

**XP fix** — Removed `is_admin=False` from `compute_all_scores()` filter. Admin accounts were being excluded from the scores dict, so `scores.get(user.id, 0.0)` always returned 0 for them.

**Honeycomb fix** — Switched to a proper flat-top hexagon (`clip-path:polygon(25% 0%,75% 0%,100% 50%,75% 100%,25% 100%,0% 50%)`). Width=72px, height=62px (correct `width × √3/2` ratio). `margin-bottom:-15px` creates the exact 25% vertical overlap. `.hive-odd` uses `margin-top:31px` (half-height) to stagger odd rows. Grid width is fixed at 296px (4 cells × 74px) so wrapping is predictable.

**WebAuthn Passkeys** — Pure Python implementation using `cbor2` + `cryptography`:
- `app/routes/passkey.py` — register/begin, register/complete, auth/begin, auth/complete, remove endpoints
- `UserPasskey` model + `passkey_enabled` column on User
- Login page rewritten with DUO logo, password form + passkey button
- Post-login prompt modal (shows once per session via `sessionStorage`) with DUO logo
- Passkey management section in settings.html (add/remove passkeys)
- `cbor2` and `cryptography` added to requirements.txt
- `PASSKEY_RP_ID` and `PASSKEY_ORIGIN` configurable via env vars

**Mail system** — Full messaging system:
- `MailMessage` model with sender/recipient, soft-delete per side
- `app/routes/mail.py` — inbox (inbox/sent folders), compose, view, delete
- `mail/inbox.html`, `mail/compose.html`, `mail/view.html` — dark theme matching platform
- Mail icon (📧) in navbar with blue unread badge, next to notification bell
- Mobile nav shows full "Messages" text link (hidden on desktop via `.mobile-only-link`)
- `mail_unread_count` injected globally via context processor
- Sends a `UserNotification` to recipient on new message

---

Same root cause as the user delete bug — ORM tries to NULL out `flag_attempts.challenge_id` instead of deleting the rows. Fix `delete_challenge` to use raw SQL first:

---

Same pattern as the user delete fix — SQLAlchemy's cascade tries to `SET challenge_id = NULL` on `flag_attempts` before deleting the challenge row, but `challenge_id` is `NOT NULL`. The fix deletes all dependent rows via raw SQL first (`flag_attempts`, `user_challenge_solves`, `challenge_opens`, `challenge_bookmarks`, `challenge_subscriptions`, `challenge_votes`), then lets the ORM delete the challenge itself cleanly.

## Conversation Summary

- **SyntaxError fix (admin.py import)**: Literal `\n` escape sequences in the import block caused a `SyntaxError`. Fixed by replacing the corrupted single-line string with a proper multi-line import.
- **XP value fix**: `compute_all_scores()` had `is_admin=False` filter, excluding admin/test accounts from the scores dict, causing XP to always show 0. Removed the `is_admin=False` filter. Also added `user_xp` (rounded raw score from `compute_all_scores()`) passed separately from `rank_percentile` via `_rank_context()` in settings.py.
- **XP display change**: Removed the yellow XP stat tile from the stats grid. XP now appears as small dim text (`0.7rem`, low opacity) below the full name / first name on both account.html and public_profile.html.
- **Honeycomb fix**: Replaced broken per-item inline style logic with proper flat-top hex CSS. Uses `clip-path:polygon(25% 0%,75% 0%,100% 50%,75% 100%,25% 100%,0% 50%)`, width=72px, height=62px, `margin-bottom:-15px` for 25% vertical overlap, `.hive-odd` with `margin-top:31px` for row stagger. Grid fixed at 296px wide (4 cells).
- **WebAuthn Passkeys**: Full implementation — `UserPasskey` model, `passkey_enabled` on User, `app/routes/passkey.py` with register/auth flows using `cbor2` + `cryptography`. Login page rewritten with DUO logo + passkey button. Post-login prompt modal (sessionStorage-dismissed). Passkey management in settings.html.
- **Mail system**: Full messaging — `MailMessage` model, `app/routes/mail.py` (inbox/sent/compose/view/delete), three templates (`mail/inbox.html`, `mail/compose.html`, `mail/view.html`). Mail icon in navbar with blue unread badge. Mobile shows full "Messages" text. `mail_unread_count` in global context processor.
- **delete_challenge NOT NULL bug**: Same ORM cascade issue as delete_user. Fixed by deleting `flag_attempts`, `user_challenge_solves`, `challenge_opens`, `challenge_bookmarks`, `challenge_subscriptions`, `challenge_votes` via raw SQL before ORM delete.

## Files and Code Summary

- **`app/routes/admin.py`**: `delete_challenge` now uses raw SQL to delete all dependent rows (flag_attempts, user_challenge_solves, challenge_opens, challenge_bookmarks, challenge_subscriptions, challenge_votes) before ORM delete. Import block fixed (was corrupted with literal `\n`).
- **`app/ranking.py`**: `compute_all_scores()` filter changed from `filter_by(is_hidden_from_scoreboard=False, is_admin=False)` to `filter_by(is_hidden_from_scoreboard=False)` — admins now included in XP calculation.
- **`app/routes/settings.py`**: `_rank_context()` now imports `compute_all_scores`, computes `user_xp = round(scores.get(user.id, 0.0))`, passes it to templates. Also imports `UserMilestone` for `user_milestones`.
- **`app/models.py`**: Added `UserPasskey` model (credential_id, public_key, sign_count, device_name), `MailMessage` model (sender_id, recipient_id, subject, body, is_read, soft-delete flags), `passkey_enabled` bool on User.
- **`app/__init__.py`**: Added `user_passkeys` and `mail_messages` table migrations, `passkey_enabled` column migration on users, `mail_unread_count` in context processor, registered `passkey_bp` and `mail_bp`, added mail/passkey endpoints to `_MOBILE_ALLOWED`.
- **`app/routes/passkey.py`**: New file — WebAuthn register/begin, register/complete, auth/begin, auth/complete, remove. Uses `cbor2` + `cryptography`. RP_ID/ORIGIN from env vars `PASSKEY_RP_ID`/`PASSKEY_ORIGIN`.
- **`app/routes/mail.py`**: New file — inbox (folder param), compose (POST sends message + UserNotification), view_message (marks read), delete_message (soft delete), unread_count API.
- **`app/templates/base.html`**: Mail icon added before notification bell (blue badge for unread). Mobile "Messages" text link with `.mobile-only-link` CSS class. Passkey prompt modal (DUO logo, shown 1.5s after load, sessionStorage dismissed). WebAuthn JS for registration in modal.
- **`app/templates/auth/login.html`**: Rewritten — dark theme, DUO logo, password form + passkey login button with full WebAuthn auth JS.
- **`app/templates/settings.html`**: Passkey management section appended — lists registered passkeys with remove buttons, add passkey button, DUO logo.
- **`app/templates/account.html`**: XP shown as small text below full name. Honeycomb CSS updated (flat-top hex, proper geometry). XP stat tile removed.
- **`app/templates/public_profile.html`**: Same XP and honeycomb changes as account.html.
- **`app/templates/mail/inbox.html`**: Two-panel layout (sidebar + message list), inbox/sent folders, unread count badge.
- **`app/templates/mail/compose.html`**: Dark compose form with To/Subject/Body fields.
- **`app/templates/mail/view.html`**: Message view with reply/delete actions.
- **`requirements.txt`**: Added `cbor2==5.6.2` and `cryptography==42.0.5`.

## Key Insights

- **NOT NULL cascade pattern**: SQLAlchemy ORM cascade tries to NULL out FK columns before deleting parent rows. Any table with `NOT NULL` FK columns (`flag_attempts.challenge_id`, `flag_attempts.user_id`, `user_challenge_solves.*`) must be deleted via raw SQL first.
- **XP = raw weighted score**: XP is the numeric output of `compute_all_scores()` — a weighted sum of solves (rarity × difficulty × points), blood bonuses, category breadth, posts, submissions, votes, reactions, comments, minus wrong attempt penalties. NOT the percentile.
- **Honeycomb geometry**: Flat-top hexagon uses `clip-path:polygon(25% 0%,75% 0%,100% 50%,75% 100%,25% 100%,0% 50%)`. Height = width × (√3/2). Vertical overlap = height × 0.25. Odd rows offset by height/2 via `margin-top`.
- **WebAuthn RP_ID**: Must match the domain serving the app. Configured via `PASSKEY_RP_ID` env var (default `localhost`) and `PASSKEY_ORIGIN` (default `http://localhost:5050`).
- **Passkey prompt**: Shows once per browser session via `sessionStorage.getItem('passkey_dismissed')`, 1.5s after page load, only when `current_user.passkey_enabled` is False.
- **DUO_LOGO.png**: Located at `app/static/img/DUO_LOGO.png`.
- **Mail soft-delete**: Messages have `is_deleted_by_sender` and `is_deleted_by_recipient` flags — messages only truly disappear when both sides delete.

## Most Recent Topic

**Topic**: Fix `delete_challenge` NOT NULL constraint error on `flag_attempts.challenge_id`

**Progress**: Fully fixed. The error was `sqlalchemy.exc.IntegrityError: NOT NULL constraint failed: flag_attempts.challenge_id` — ORM tried to SET `challenge_id=NULL` on flag_attempts rows before deleting the challenge. Applied the same raw SQL pre-deletion pattern used for `delete_user`.

**Tools Used**:
- **fsReplace on `app/routes/admin.py`**: Replaced `delete_challenge` route body to add a raw SQL block using `db.engine.connect()` that deletes from `flag_attempts`, `user_challenge_solves`, `challenge_opens`, `challenge_bookmarks`, `challenge_subscriptions`, `challenge_votes` WHERE `challenge_id=:c` before calling `db.session.delete(challenge)` and `db.session.commit()`.
